## Where we are right now

V1 web surface is **functionally complete**. Pre-launch sprint closed 2026-05-13 (19 iterations). 2026-05-14 then landed **28 PRs** across two waves.

**2026-06-21 — feat(seating): 3D seating lab — flag-gated R3F prototype (PR pending, auto-merge).** Owner direction: make the seat plan feel "like a game where you move things around." Built a **flag-gated (`NEXT_PUBLIC_SEATING_3D`), READ-ONLY** React-Three-Fiber prototype on a throwaway `…/seating/lab` route (404 when off; never touches the 2D editor; no writes). Renders the couple's REAL tables/floor/guests/mood-palette as a navigable 3D room: Build mode (tap-select, drag-to-slide with game-feel, tap-floor to drop a table), Play mode (tap a guest → avatar walks from the entrance around the tables to their chair), palette-driven lighting/materials + live switcher, glassmorphism HUD. Pure `lib/seating-3d.ts` (no three.js → server-safe) + `dynamic(ssr:false)` client loader + the R3F scene. New deps `@react-three/fiber@9.6` + `@react-three/drei@10.7` (three@0.184 already present — the reveal uses raw three). Adversarial 6-dimension/32-agent review → 8 verified findings, all fixed (touch tap-to-drop, drag soft-lock on pointercancel/blur, synthetic-click-after-drag guard, rotation-sign parity with rendered chairs, null-position grid fallback, removed-seat-aware auto-seat, perf: DPR/shadow-res/shared geometry). v2 upgrades documented: GLTF character + NavMesh + instancing + post-processing. tsc 0 · `next lint` clean; CI production build is the gate (R3F is client-only + dynamically imported). SPEC IMPACT None (additive flag-off prototype) → CHANGELOG + DECISION_LOG + `0008_Seating_AS_BUILT` lineage.
**2026-06-21 — feat(seating): linked tables group as ONE + full-screen editor (PR pending, auto-merge).** Owner ask — "when we link seats, they will be grouped as one… so when we rotate a table, it rotates as one… like how Keynote groups shapes. and break apart will unlink them," plus declutter the seating page. Tables sharing `link_group_id` now move and rotate as one rigid unit (drag translates the whole unit; the ±15°/Flip buttons, the desktop rotate-handle, and the two-finger twist all orbit each member around the unit centroid + spin its own angle by the same delta, via a px round-trip so a non-square canvas can't shear it). Group rotate persists positions+angles together (coherent on reload); group move persists on Save. "Break apart" = the existing unlink, relabeled throughout. NO schema/migration, NO server-action behavior change — pure client rigid-body geometry on the existing link (seating math stays per-table). Also removed the seating hero title + description so the editor fills the screen (stats + Walkthrough link → one compact bar; sr-only h1 kept). ⚠ Reverses the 2026-06-10 "link = identity + QR only" lock (owner-authorized 2026-06-21). tsc 0 (only pre-existing unrelated `paper`/`archiver` errors); `next lint` clean on all 3 files; CI build + Vercel preview are the runtime gate (no local env on disk). **2026-06-13 — feat(pax): adaptive pax pricing — Phase 1 schema (no behavior change).** Owner feature threading one guest count from the guest list → vendor inquiries → per-vendor pricing → budget; designed + locked 2026-06-13 (6 decisions, `DECISION_LOG.md` "Adaptive Pax Pricing"). Model: `events.estimated_pax` = the minimum-pax floor; `live_pax = max(floor, sure-attending headcount)`; past the floor vendors get the count + couple sees "prices may change"; vendor sets an optional per-added-guest rate (blank = none); count fully live but confirmed cost changes go through a symmetric vendor confirm; couple view realtime-by-default; auto-finalize at the guest-list edit deadline. Migration `20261211000000` adds NULL-safe columns to `events` / `vendor_services` / `chat_threads` / `event_vendors` — ⚠ NOT yet applied to prod (apply when Phase 2 reads them). KEY: the vendor per-pax model (0022 §2.2) + cost-delta flow (0021 §12.3) were spec'd-but-unbuilt, so we're building the spec. Phases 2-6 (couple meter · inquiry snapshot · vendor field · push+recompute · HQ audit) queued. tsc/lint/build unaffected (no TS). SPEC IMPACT → DECISION_LOG + memory.

(3) the deferred lifecycle is now built: a branch's status is **derived from its latest activation order** (paid + in the 28-day `orders.expires_at` window → Active; past it → **Expired**; unpaid → Pending), so **auto-lapse is automatic at read time — no cron** ([[cron-free]]); plus a one-tap **Renew** (`renewBranch` → fresh ₱999 apply-then-pay → admin approval reactivates with a new window). Shipped the foundation only: pure **`lib/budget-allocation.ts`** (`computeBudgetAllocation` — median→proportion→₱ spine · fixed-then-proportion · cushion/slack-first · soft-floor-warn · p25–p75 band · `surplusMode` park|distribute) + Layer-1 capture migration **`20260824000000_budget_allocation_decisions`** (couple-own-only RLS · **admins no blanket read by design** · RA 10173 erasable). `tsc`+`lint` green · runtime harness **20/20** (the worked example reproduces exactly). **⚠ Migration NOT applied** — `db push` would co-apply the owner's pending `20260817` monogram migration, and the version was renamed off a remote-only `20260823` collision (vendor_self_comp_caps); ships ahead of application (nothing consumes it yet). **2026-06-04 — demo seed images from a small Picsum pool (so demo photos load).** "Why are there no photos?" The seed gave every vendor a unique `picsum.photos/…/800/600` image; ~4,900 unique large requests rate-limited Picsum → all failed. Fix: pool the URLs — `snl${i%40}` (≈40 logos @400×300) + `snp${(i*4+j)%60}` (≈60 photos @600×400), reused everywhere → browser caches ~100 images, Picsum stops throttling. **Owner action: tap Create demo vendors again to re-seed with pooled URLs.** `tsc`+`lint` green. **SPEC IMPACT: none.**

Added `failedLogos` + `onError` → falls back to the initials tile instead of a broken icon (host-agnostic). Root follow-up (separate): shrink the seed's picsum sizes + re-Create so real photos load. `tsc`+`lint` green. **SPEC IMPACT: none.**

**2026-06-04 — vendor-pick badge distortion: real fix (rename collision class) (0021).** The #908 portal didn't resolve it (badge still ballooned with the `.pbacc .v` signature — likely stale PWA JS, and the portal was fragile). Root, source-level fix: the overlay badge was `className="badge v"`, so the accordion's card rule `.pbacc .v {min-height:300px;flex:1 1 auto;flex-direction:column}` matched it by the `v` class alone. Renamed badge modifiers `v→vrf`, `b→bst` (CSS+JSX) so `.pbacc .v` can never match — immune to nesting/portal/specificity. Hardened `.csov .r .badge` (`flex:0 0 auto;min-height:0`) too. `tsc`+`lint` green. **SPEC IMPACT: none.** (Owner tip: full-reload the app — old cached JS won't show the fix.)

**2026-06-04 — stop unexpected mobile zoom (native-app feel · 0000).** Owner: *"screen sometimes zooms in unexpectedly … we want it to feel like an app."* CSS-only hardening in `globals.css` (unlayered, so it beats Tailwind utilities): a `pointer: coarse` 16px floor on `input/select/textarea` kills iOS focus-zoom (root cause — inputs `font: inherit` shrink to 14px inside `text-sm` wrappers and Safari zooms in on focus); `html { touch-action: manipulation }` drops double-tap-zoom + the 300ms delay; `html { overscroll-behavior: none }` removes the pull-to-refresh bounce. Pinch-zoom left **enabled** (`maximumScale: 5`, WCAG 1.4.4). Viewport + manifest were already correct (no change). **SPEC IMPACT: none.** No owner action.

Fixed across the three weak points — try/catch around the commit (unwind + show the existing retry error on reject) + a hard-`window.location.assign` watchdog if the client router wedges or `router.push` no-ops + a 2s `AbortController` on the awaited PostHog `captureEvent` fetch (it could drag the serverless function to its timeout) + the post-insert shortlist/anchor seed wrapped non-fatal (a throw there rejected the commit *after* the event existed → duplicate-on-retry). typecheck + lint green. SPEC IMPACT none. Follow-up flagged: the commit is still non-idempotent on the other failure branches (needs a client idempotency key + server dedup).

| Item | The decision | Effort once decided |
|---|---|---|
| **Save-the-Date render pipeline** | Browser-canvas + MediaRecorder (free, ~1 day) OR server FFmpeg (needs Workers Paid plan + Hetzner VM pool, ~3 days) | 1–3 days |
| **Panood (live stream)** | Provision Cloudflare Stream Live + YouTube Data API + master `@SetnayanWeddings` channel | 5–7 days |
| **Marketplace commission model** | Free-listing forever / commission per booking / paid tier — pick before launch advertising | Pricing call only |
| **Daily.co video meetings (0019)** | Sign up + paste API key | 2 days code |
| **Anthropic Claude API (0032 Contract Intelligence)** | Sign up + spend cap → unblocks paid SKU | 3 days code |
| **Apple Developer Program** | $99/yr enrollment | 2-5 day approval; signed `.dmg` + future iOS Papic |
| **Render pipeline infra** | Cloudflare Workers Paid ($5/mo) + Hetzner Cloud VMs (€15/mo) — shared by 0011 / 0012 / 0017 / 0024 | 2 days code once provisioned |
| **Public website visual redesign** | Owner provides direction on what to change. Current state (post PR #21): split-CTA hero + trust signals + pricing table + compact roadmap — functional but generic. Owner queued this for a later session — needs a specific brief ("hero feels weak", "want a hero image not a device mock", "needs a how-it-works section", etc.) before code can ship | 0.5–2 days depending on scope |
| **Monogram tier system + AI-automated Bespoke flow (queued for new session)** | Owner locked the 3-tier model + Bespoke pricing + UX rules 2026-05-14 (reference images shared). **Free / Basic**: 2 letters + `&` (e.g. `J & S`), 1-2 default fonts, simple geometric frame. **Pro (₱99 widget upgrade per 0004)**: 2 letters OR full names, ornamental + heritage frames, 8+ premium fonts. **Bespoke (₱2,999, NEW SKU)**: AI-generated interlocked letterforms — DALL-E 3 HD behind the scenes, branded as **"Setnayan AI"** in all customer-facing copy (DALL-E never named in the UI). Replaces the old `Custom Monogram Pack — remove watermark` SKU. **CUSTOMER UX (in-app, live render — no external tools)**: (1) Guided brief form: initials/names + 3 personality words + motif preference + style direction + **reference image upload area** for couples to share inspiration. (2) Pay ₱2,999. (3) App fires the first generation server-side — DALL-E 3 HD × 4 variations stash to R2 — customer sees live thumbnails in ~30 sec. (4) **Refinement loop, up to 30 re-renders included in the SKU**: customer types text feedback ("more delicate", "more gold", "swap wreath for crest") + each refinement re-fires DALL-E with the SAME locked brief + appended feedback. Counter visible: "X refinements left." (5) After 30 re-renders OR customer hits "Accept final": top result auto-vectorizes via vectorizer.ai → SVG goes live event-wide. **🔴 ANTI-ABUSE RULE**: the brief inputs (initials/names/connector) **lock after the first generation** and cannot be edited. Re-renders REFINE the existing concept; they do NOT restart from scratch. This prevents 1 transaction → multiple distinct logos (e.g., logo for self + logo for sister + logo for friend). **Optional add-on SKU (V2)**: `+10 re-renders` pack at ₱199 (multi-buy allowed) if a customer exhausts their quota. **Cost ceiling**: 30 × $0.08 HD = ~₱135 max per customer; avg ~₱45 (most use 5-15 rerenders) → 95% margin at ₱2,999. **Owner signups needed**: OpenAI Platform (`OPENAI_API_KEY`), Vectorizer.ai (`VECTORIZER_API_KEY`). **Branding**: all UI strings say "Setnayan AI" not "DALL-E" or "OpenAI"; server-side calls only; no API key in client bundle | 5-7 days code once API keys are in Vercel |

## Locked architectural decisions (no further owner input needed)

### Time-limited services — **no cron**

For services with a paid time budget (Panood live stream, Papic camera-seat session, future limited-duration SKUs), use database-state + on-access checks. Owner locked 2026-05-14: no Vercel Cron, no Supabase `pg_cron`, no Cloudflare Cron Triggers.

**Pattern:**
- `service_sessions` row stores `scheduled_for`, `start_window_opens` (= `scheduled_for - 30 min`), `start_window_closes` (= `scheduled_for + 2 hours`), `duration_minutes`, `started_at`, `expires_at`, `status`
- Couple hits **Start** between `start_window_opens` and `start_window_closes` → server sets `started_at = now()`, `expires_at = now() + duration_minutes`, flips status to `active`
- Every read of the service surface validates `now() < expires_at` server-side; flips status to `expired` lazily on next access if exceeded
- Client tracks the countdown locally from `expires_at` for the visible timer; polls every 30 sec to revalidate
- When countdown hits 0 client-side, UI swaps to "session ended" state immediately
- **Resource teardown** (stopping the Cloudflare Stream broadcast, releasing Papic seats, etc.): hybrid client-driven + lazy admin sweep:
  - **Client-driven (primary)**: countdown hits 0 → client fires `/api/sessions/[id]/teardown` → server calls the external API (Cloudflare, etc.) to stop the resource
  - **Lazy sweep (backup)**: any couple/admin page load sweeps `WHERE expires_at < now() AND status = 'active'` and fires teardown — covers the case where the broadcaster's browser is offline

Applies to: 0011 Panood, 0012 Papic, future time-budgeted SKUs. **Does NOT** apply to bookings or events themselves (those use absolute date scheduling).

## Stack quick-reference

- **Repo:** https://github.com/iscasasola/setnayan-platform (public, AGPL-3.0)
- **Hosting:** Vercel (Hobby plan), auto-deploys from `main`
- **Domain:** `setnayan.com` (Vercel-managed SSL)
- **DB:** Supabase (Singapore region) — **31 migrations on main as of EOD 2026-05-14** (last 6 are unpushed to prod, see Owner-side blockers)
- **Storage:** Cloudflare R2 — 4 PH-region buckets (live writes from PR #18), plus Supabase Storage for the `platform-assets` bucket (legacy)
- **Email:** Resend — domain `setnayan.com` verified, `noreply@setnayan.com` from-address, **9 of 10 V1 transactional templates wired**
- **Observability:** Sentry (errors) + PostHog (3 funnel events) + 3 Supabase-side funnels at `/admin/funnels` (signup→event→paid order, vendor signup→profile→booking, week-over-week)
- **Native:** Tauri 2 desktop wrapper (unsigned macOS .dmg on GitHub Releases v0.0.1); iOS/Android deferred to V1.0+
